      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses in the 6th century
       </b>
       . During the period 501 to 600 there were 251
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 93 were partial, 87 were annular (one
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 65 were total, and 6 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was four, occurring in 17 different years: 506, 517, 524, 528, 535, 539, 542, 546, 553, 557, 564, 571, 575, 582, 586, 593, and 596. Three months, August 528, July 539, and May 542 had two eclipses.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Dates are given using the
       <a href="/wiki/Julian_calendar" title="Julian calendar">
        Julian calendar
       </a>
       .
      </p>
